SOV_stalins_paranoia = {

	SOV_falsify_evidence = {

		icon = eng_trade_unions_support

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_nkvd_cooldown
			}
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {

				}
			}

		icon = {
			key = SOV_garrison_none
			trigger = {
				229 = { check_variable = { var = SOV_garrison_strength value = 1 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = SOV_garrison_weak
			trigger = {
				229 = {
					check_variable = { var = SOV_garrison_strength value = 2 compare = equals }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = SOV_garrison_strong
			trigger = {
				229 = {
					check_variable = { var = SOV_garrison_strength value = 3 compare = equals }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = SOV_garrison_total
			trigger = {
				229 = { check_variable = { var = SOV_garrison_strength value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { 
				 state = 229 }}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view 

		available = {
			if = {
				NOT = {
					229 = { check_variable = { var = SOV_garrison_strength value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 2169 }
				has_equipment = { horse_equipment > 724 }
				has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 89 }
				has_equipment = { anti_tank_equipment > 42 }
				has_equipment = { field_gun_equipment > 19 }
				has_equipment = { heavy_artillery_equipment > 19 }
				has_equipment = { anti_air_equipment > 17 }
				has_equipment = { support_equipment > 213 }
				has_equipment = { motorized_equipment > 40 }
				has_equipment = { radio_equipment > 99 }				
			}
		}

SOV_GER_evacuations_category = {
	SOV_evacuate_lwow = {
		name = "Lwów Evacuation"
		activation = {
			SOV = {
				has_war_with = GER 
			}
		}
		available = {
			SOV = {
				NOT = {
					controls_state = 91
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		icon = generic_construction
		highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { 
				 state = 91 
			}
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_industry_relocation_new_tt 
			
		
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					91 = {
						OR = {
							arms_factory > 0
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						91 = {
							arms_factory > 0
						}
					}
					91 = {
						remove_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
						}
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 40 
								state = 404
								state = 732
								state = 742
								state = 654
								state = 590
								state = 589
								state = 581

							}
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
							}
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						91 = {
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
					}
					91 = {
						remove_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
						}
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 40 
								state = 404
								state = 732
								state = 742
								state = 654
								state = 590
								state = 589
								state = 581

							}
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
							}
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			GER =  {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_1
					amount = 1500
					producer = SOV
				}	

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 75
					producer = SOV
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = radio_equipment
					amount = 75
					producer = SOV
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment_1
					amount = 150
					producer = SOV
				}
			}
		}

	}

			}

					SOV = { has_full_control_of_state = 219 }
				}
				219 = { #Mowscow

						type = anti_air_building
						level = 8
					}					
				}
				219 = { #Mowscow
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 15
						province = {
							id = 6350
							level < 14
						}
					}
				}				
			}
			add_resource = {
				state = 219
				amount = 20
				type = steel
			}				
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}

					limit = {
						has_tech = sov_heavy_fighter_1938
						NOT = {
							has_tech = sov_heavy_fighter_1940		
						}	
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = heavy_fighter_equipment_1938
							amount = 200
							producer = SOV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = sov_heavy_fighter_1940
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = heavy_fighter_equipment_1940
							amount = 200
							producer = SOV
					}	
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = sov_1939_medium_tank_chassis
						NOT = {
							has_tech = sov_1940_heavy_tank_chassis
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = medium_tank_chassis
							amount = 500
							producer = SOV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = sov_1940_heavy_tank_chassis
						NOT = {
							has_tech = sov_1939_medium_tank_chassis
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = heavy_tank_chassis
							amount = 350
							producer = SOV
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = sov_1940_heavy_tank_chassis
						has_tech = sov_1939_medium_tank_chassis
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = heavy_tank_chassis
							amount = 350
							producer = SOV
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = medium_tank_chassis
							amount = 500
							producer = SOV
					}
				}
			}	
		}	
	}

	SOV_2_5_year_plan_mission = {

		icon = generic_construction

		available = {
			check_variable = { var = progress_5_year_plan value = 100 compare = greater_than_or_equals }						
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 770

		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			tag = SOV
		}

		activation = {
			OR = { 
				date > 1936.01.01
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_idea_2_5_year_plan			
		
			SOV = { country_event = { days = 1 id = soviet.119 } }
			set_variable = {
				var = progress_5_year_plan
				value = 0
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}		

		complete_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_idea_2_5_year_plan 				

			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.2

			SOV = { country_event = { days = 1 id = soviet.118 } }			

 			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_5_year_plan_3_tt   	
			set_variable = {
				var = progress_5_year_plan
				value = 0
			}
		}	
	}

	SOV_plan_state_marking = {
 		icon = generic_industry
 		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
 		}
		visible = {
		}
		activation = {
			SOV = {
				has_idea = SOV_idea_2_5_year_plan
			}
		} 
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
 		days_mission_timeout = 79
		days_remove = 80
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_idea = SOV_idea_2_5_year_plan
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = SOV_plan_state_marking			
				}
			}	
			SOV = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_state_flag = SOV_5_year_plan_IC }
						NOT = { has_state_flag = SOV_gulag_economy_flag }
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 4
							include_locked = yes
						}
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 4
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = SOV_5_year_plan_IC 
					custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_5_year_plan_1_tt
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = progress_5_year_plan value = 2 }
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_defensive_war = yes
					NOT = {
						has_idea = SOV_idea_2_5_year_plan
					}
				}
			} 
		}
 	}
